### [168] [From Brewing to Resolution: Tracing the Internal Lifecycle of Code Reasoning in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17648)
*Siyue Chen,Yifu Guo,Yuquan Lu,Zishan Xu,Jiaye Lin,Jianbo Lin,Siyu Zhang,Cheng Yang,Junxin Li,Yujia Li,Yu Huo,Ruixuan Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文提出了一种双诊断框架（层间线性探针+上下文剥离解码），揭示了LLM在代码推理任务中先"酝酿"答案再分化为四种解决结果（解决、过度处理、错误解决、未解决）的内部生命周期，发现酝酿脚手架在不同模型间稳定存在，但解决成功率随能力/规模/训练变化，整体解决率仅41.5%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准准确率指标无法解释LLM为何能处理变量追踪但在语义等价的循环任务上失败，因此需要更深层的内部诊断方法来理解模型推理的生命周期和失败模式。

Method: 提出双诊断框架：1）层间线性探针（layer-wise linear probing）追踪答案的可恢复性；2）上下文剥离解码（Context-Stripped Decoding, CSD）检测答案的可自解码性。将推理生命周期分为酝酿阶段和四种解决结果。

Result: 在6个代码推理任务族、16个模型（Qwen/Llama/DeepSeek）上验证：整体解决率仅41.5%，多项任务低于30%；酝酿时长稳定在24-42%之间；Function Call任务随调用深度从1到3，解决率从61.1%骤降至2.5%。

Conclusion: 酝酿脚手架（brewing scaffold）是跨Decoder-only Transformer家族的稳定经验规律，而解决成功率随模型能力、规模和训练变化。表面准确率掩盖了本质上不同的失败模式，需要更细粒度的诊断。

Abstract: Standard accuracy metrics cannot explain why LLMs handle variable tracking but fail on semantically equivalent loops. We study an internal lifecycle of code reasoning in which models first brew the answer, making it linearly recoverable many layers before it becomes self-decodable, and then diverge into one of four resolution outcomes: Resolved, Overprocessed, Misresolved, or Unresolved. Understanding this lifecycle matters because similar task accuracies can mask fundamentally different failure modes that surface-level evaluation cannot detect. We introduce a dual diagnostic framework pairing layer-wise linear probing with Context-Stripped Decoding (CSD) and apply it to six code-reasoning task families across 16 models spanning Qwen, Llama, and DeepSeek architectures. All four outcomes carry substantial mass in every task family: overall Resolved is only 41.5%, with multiple tasks below 30%. Controlled sweeps over structure, depth, and operators expose task-specific failure bottlenecks: Function Call Resolved plunges from 61.1% to 2.5% as call depth increases from one to three. Across architectures and scales, the brewing scaffold remains stable, with normalized brewing duration 24-42% across all 16 models, while resolution success varies with capability. This indicates that the scaffold is a stable empirical regularity across the tested decoder-only Transformer families, whereas resolution success covaries with capability, scale, and training. Code: https://github.com/euyis1019/llm-brewing

</details>


### [169] [Using Cognitive Models to Improve Language Model Simulation of Human Persuasion Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17657)
*Zirui Cheng,Zeyu Shen,Thomas L. Griffiths,Peter Henderson*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文提出"方程到行为提示"方法，引导大语言模型模拟人类决策中的认知模型（如贝叶斯更新、动机推理等），并在此基础上通过强化学习训练小模型，使其信念误差降低26.5%，并能在说服游戏中提升平均信念变化2.5%–12%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型的安全评估和训练中使用的模拟人类数据往往无法涵盖人类决策行为的多样性（如贝叶斯更新、动机推理等认知偏差），需要更系统的方法来模拟真实人类的决策方式。

Method: 提出Equation-to-Behavior Prompting方法，利用认知科学和经济学中的数学模型（贝叶斯更新、仿射扭曲、动机更新、Grether的α-β模型）引导大语言模型模拟人类决策；针对小模型，进一步使用强化学习（Equation-to-Behavior RL）来训练其遵循数学规则。

Result: 大模型能通过提示匹配基于方程的认知模型，小模型失败；但使用强化学习训练后，小模型在分布外参数化下信念误差降低26.5%；考虑多样化决策者的训练使平均信念变化比纯贝叶斯训练提升2.5%–12%（即使在对GPT-5-mini进行说服时）。

Conclusion: 该方法可改善AI安全评估和训练中的人类模拟，使其更真实多样；同时为研究更复杂的人类决策数学模型提供了新工具。

Abstract: People make decisions differently in strategic interactions. Some update beliefs like a Bayesian; others exhibit biases like motivated reasoning. Although creators of large language models use simulated humans for safety evaluations and training, they often fail to cover this breadth of human behavior. We argue that cognitive science and economics provide a convenient tool for doing so, making use of mathematical models of human decision-making. We propose an approach that we call Equation-to-Behavior Prompting for guiding large language models to match cognitive models, and evaluate this approach on persuasion games based on legal decision-making. We find that large models can approximate equation-based specifications -- Bayesian updating, affine distortion, motivated updating, and Grether's $α$-$β$ model -- using prompting, but small models fail to do so. However, training small models with reinforcement learning to adhere to mathematical rules, Equation-to-Behavior RL, reduces belief error by 26.5% in out-of-distribution parameterizations. We show that these simulations can help create diverse training environments; training small models to consider different kinds of decision-makers improves average belief change by 2.5%--12% over Bayesian-only training, even when persuading GPT-5-mini. Our work could improve human simulations for training and evaluation in increasingly realistic settings, and could also enable novel research into more complicated mathematical models of human decision-making.

</details>

Abstract: As LLM-based shopping agents enter production, existing benchmarks fail to capture how a shopper's requirements arrive: stated implicitly in the query, recorded in a profile, or revealed only when the right question is asked. To address this gap, we introduce EComAgentBench, a benchmark of 662 tasks grounded in real Amazon products and reviews. ### [173] [Shattering the Autoregressive Curse: Dynamic Epistemic Entropy Orchestrated Erasable Reinforcement Learning for LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17735)
*Ziliang Wang,Kang An,Faqiang Qian,Jialu Cai,Cijun Ouyang,Yuhang Wang,Qibing Ren,Yichao Wu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出动态 epistemic 熵编排可擦除强化学习（E³RL），通过将模型内生局部自回归交叉熵作为 epistemic 不确定性的内在坐标，引入分段级自适应动态阈值和优势分配，使模型能够精确切除局部逻辑缺陷并复用历史 KV 缓存流，从而赋予推理过程自愈能力，打破长序列推理中的自回归诅咒。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 RL 扩展了 LLM 认知边界，但在长程逻辑推理中容易受到自回归诅咒的影响：早期的小 epistemic 扰动沿 MDP 流不可逆传播，引发级联故障，导致推理轨迹崩溃。需要一种方法克服这种单个早期错误会损害后续所有推理步骤的自回归级联问题。

Method: E³RL 的核心方法包括：(1) 将模型内生的局部自回归交叉熵作为 epistemic 不确定性的内在坐标，消除对外部信号的依赖；(2) 引入分段级自适应动态阈值和优势分配机制；(3) 支持精确切除局部逻辑缺陷，同时复用历史 KV 缓存流，赋予自愈能力。

Result: 在 DeepMath-103k 数据集上训练。E³RL 重塑了长序列推理的探索效率，提升了样本效率，同时保持线性内存开销。在 AIME 等数学推理基准上，4B 参数模型超越此前 SOTA 5.349%，8B 模型超越 6.514%。

Conclusion: E³RL 打破了长序列推理中的自回归诅咒，为下一代自愈型通用人工智能奠定了理论和系统级基础。

Abstract: Although reinforcement learning (RL) has expanded the cognitive boundaries of large language models (LLMs), it often remains vulnerable to the autoregressive curse in long-horizon logical reasoning: small epistemic perturbations introduced early in generation can propagate irreversibly along the Markov decision process flow, triggering cascading failures that drive the reasoning trajectory toward collapse. To overcome this autoregressive cascade, in which a single early mistake can compromise all subsequent reasoning steps, we propose dynamic epistemic entropy orchestrated erasable reinforcement learning ($\text{E}^3\text{RL}$). $\text{E}^3\text{RL}$ eliminates reliance on external signals by grounding the model's endogenous local autoregressive cross-entropy as an intrinsic coordinate of epistemic uncertainty. By introducing segment-level adaptive dynamic thresholds and advantage allocation, $\text{E}^3\text{RL}$ enables the model to precisely excise localized logical defects while reusing historical key-value (KV) cache streams, thereby endowing the reasoning process with a self-healing capability. We train $\text{E}^3\text{RL}$ on the DeepMath-103k dataset. Experimental results show that $\text{E}^3\text{RL}$ reshapes the exploration efficiency of long-sequence reasoning and improves sample efficiency while maintaining linear memory overhead. On mathematical reasoning benchmarks such as AIME, $\text{E}^3\text{RL}$ achieves substantial performance gains, with the 4B and 8B parameter models surpassing previous state-of-the-art (SOTA) results by 5.349\% and 6.514\%, respectively. These findings suggest that $\text{E}^3\text{RL}$ shatters the autoregressive curse in long-sequence reasoning and establishes a theoretical and systems-level foundation for the next generation of self-healing artificial general intelligence (AGI).

### [174] [DecoSearch: Complexity-Aware Routing and Plan-Level Repair for Text-to-SQL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17821)
*Esteban Schafir,Xu Zheng,Hojat Allah Salehi,Zhuomin Chen,Mo Sha,Wei Cheng,Dongsheng Luo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: DecoSearch 是一个无需训练、模型无关的框架，通过动态路由将复杂NL2SQL任务分解为DAG子问题，结合模式选择、判断器、RAG和拓扑优化，在BIRD和Spider上达到SOTA水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM在复杂、需要多步数据感知推理的SQL生成任务上表现不佳，且现有方法缺乏灵活调整推理难度的能力。

Method: DecoSearch包含：(1) Schema Selector剪枝无关模式；(2) LLM Judger判断是否需要对问题进行分解；(3) 简单问题直接生成，复杂问题构建DAG子问题图；(4) RAG组件提供相似示例支持；(5) Topology Refiner在执行失败时修正分解拓扑结构。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated remarkable capabilities in translating natural language to SQL, yet existing methods still falter on complex queries requiring multi-step, data-aware reasoning. We introduce DecoSearch, a training-free framework that addresses this by routing each query to the appropriate level of reasoning effort. A lightweight Schema Selector first prunes the full database schema to the relevant tables and columns. An LLM Judger then decides whether the question requires decomposition: straightforward questions follow a direct generation path and complex ones are escalated to a Directed Acyclic Graph (DAG) of atomic sub-questions, each solved by a targeted SQL generation step. A RAG component grounds the decomposer with semantically similar training examples, and a Topology Refiner restructures the reasoning plan when execution failures signal a flawed decomposition rather than a fixable SQL error. DecoSearch achieves 70.53% execution accuracy on BIRD and 88.31% on Spider with a DeepSeek backbone, surpassing all training-free baselines while consuming an order of magnitude fewer tokens than competing methods. It also functions as a model-agnostic wrapper, consistently improving fine-tuned SQL generation backbones without any modification to the pipeline.

### [176] [A homotopy-type-theoretic generalization of neurosymbolic inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17851)
*Fernando Zhapa-Camacho,Robert Hoehndorf*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出用同伦类型论替换集合论，构建神经符号系统的统一框架，将传统加权模型计数泛化为信念加权同伦基数，能自然处理对称性和多证明信息，通过对称群平均实现捷径感知的概念后验，在MNIST基准上单模型集成即优于多样性集成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有神经符号系统基于集合论，但集合会遗忘两类重要信息：(1) σ-结构在理论对称性下等价；(2) 查询存在多个不同证明。这种信息丢失导致推理捷径问题，需要复杂的集成或密度估计方法才能处理。

Method: 将底层集合替换为同伦类型论中的类型，把原功能函数转化为信念加权同伦基数。同伦基数计数时每个对象按其对称性倒数计数，保留对称性和多证明信息。通过对称群平均，得到混淆集单纯形中唯一的对称不变点，作为捷径感知的概念后验。

Result: 证明了保守性定理：当对称性平凡时，恢复经典功能函数。在MNIST推理捷径基准上，单模型对称平均方法在标定上优于多样性集成，同时保持标签准确率和概念可识别性不变。

Conclusion: 该框架统一了多种神经符号系统，揭示了推理捷径背后的对称性本质，提供了一种无需集成或密度估计的封闭形式解决方案，代码已开源。

Abstract: A wide range of neurosymbolic (NeSy) systems compute one functional: a belief-weighted sum of a logical quantity over a space of $σ$-structures, of which weighted model counting, fuzzy logic, and probabilistic logic are special cases. This account is built on sets, and a set deliberately forgets two things that are important for NeSy: when two $σ$-structures are the same up to a symmetry of the theory, and how many distinct proofs witness a query. Replacing the underlying sets by types, in the sense of homotopy type theory, preserves this information, and turns this functional into a belief-weighted homotopy cardinality, a notion of size that counts each object in inverse proportion to its symmetries. We develop the framework from scratch for NeSy systems, prove a conservativity theorem that recovers the classical functional when symmetries are trivial, and show that the symmetry our framework exposes is exactly the one behind reasoning shortcuts. The payoff is concrete: the shortcut-aware concept posterior that recent methods reach by ensembling or expressive density estimation is the only symmetry-invariant point of the confusion-set simplex, computable in closed form by averaging a single model over the symmetry group. On MNIST reasoning-shortcut benchmarks this single-model wrapper is better calibrated than a diversity-trained ensemble, while leaving label accuracy and identifiable concepts untouched. Code is freely available at https://github.com/bio-ontology-research-group/hott-nesy.

### [177] [FlowRAG: Synergizing Explicit Reasoning via Frequency-Aware Multi-Granularity Graph Flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17856)
*Bihao Zhan,Zongsheng Cao,Jie Zhou,Bo Zhang,Liang He*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: FlowRAG 提出了一种基于四层异构图（段落、摘要、句子、实体）的语义感知检索增强框架，通过双粒度激活和频率加权流模块，在复杂推理任务上达到SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 GraphRAG 方法基于实体图构建，存在两个问题：(i) 当用户查询抽象、语义稀疏时检索不足；(ii) 多跳推理脆弱，噪声激活导致实体间过渡偏差，破坏推理链可靠性。

Method: (1) 构建四层异构图（段落-摘要-句子-实体），摘要节点作为粗粒度语义枢纽；(2) 双粒度激活模块（摘要-查询对齐 + 句子级匹配）增强语义召回；(3) 频率加权流模块，通过段落内词频加权实体-段落链接，修剪噪声，提取高置信度推理路径作为显式逻辑骨架。

Result: 在复杂推理基准上取得了 state-of-the-art 性能。

Conclusion: FlowRAG 通过语义感知的检索框架有效提升了语义召回和显式推理能力，解决了现有 GraphRAG 在抽象查询和多跳推理上的不足。

Abstract: Graph-based retrieval-augmented generation (GraphRAG) is effective for knowledge-intensive and multi-hop query tasks; however, many existing methods primarily seed entity-based graphs and rely on implicit semantic relevance propagation. This often (i) under-retrieves when user queries are abstract and semantically sparse at the entity level, and (ii) suffers from brittle multi-hop reasoning, where noisy activations can derail entity-to-entity transitions and corrupt the inferred relation chain, yielding unreliable conclusions. To this end, we propose \texttt{FlowRAG}, a semantic-aware retrieval framework that improves both semantic recall and explicit reasoning. Specifically, \texttt{FlowRAG} constructs a quad-level heterogeneous graph over passages, summaries, sentences, and entities, where summary nodes serve as a coarse semantic hub. At retrieval time, a dual-granularity activation module combines summary--query alignment with sentence-level matching to activate relevant entities under paraphrase and abstraction robustly. We then introduce a frequency-aware weighted flow module that routes relevance through entity--passage links weighted by within-passage term frequency, pruning noisy connections and extracting high-confidence reasoning paths as an explicit logic skeleton for generation. Extensive experiments show that \texttt{FlowRAG} obtains state-of-the-art performance on complex reasoning benchmarks.

### [178] [StepGuard: Guarding Web Navigation via Single-Step Calibration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17871)
*Zhihao Cui,Yuchen Zhang,Xiyang Sun,Yaxiong Wang,Li Zhu,Jinpeng Hu,Liu Liu,Mengjia Li,Yujiao Wu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出StepGuard框架，通过动态双策略优化（DDPO）解决奖励冲突，以及置信度引导的自适应导航反思（CANR）校准单步误差，在Web导航任务上达到SOTA性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Web导航方法因奖励错配和错误传播导致单步决策脆弱，奖励冲突（导航优先 vs 答案优先）未被有效解耦。

Method: 1. DDPO：动态切换导航优先模式和答案优先模式，缓解奖励冲突；2. CANR：估计每步置信度，仅在必要时触发反思，利用对比奖励鼓励自我纠正；3. 整体框架StepGuard整合上述组件。

Result: 在标准Web导航基准上显著提升导航与答案准确率，达到新SOTA。

Conclusion: 单步校准（动态策略优化+置信度引导反思）有效提升了Web导航的鲁棒性和准确性。

Abstract: Web navigation requires agents to follow natural language goals, interact with web pages, and produce accurate answers. While recent advances leverage vision-language models and reinforcement learning, existing methods still suffer from single-step fragility due to reward misalignment and error propagation. To tackle the reward entanglement, we design Dynamic Dual-Policy Optimization (DDPO), which dynamically switches between a navigation-first mode for exploration and an answer-first mode for question-answering to mitigate reward conflict. To calibrate the single-step error, we propose Confidence-Guided Adaptive Navigation Reflection (CANR), a mechanism that estimates per-step confidence, triggers reflection only when necessary, and uses contrastive rewards to encourage self-correction to calibrate the single-step inaccuracy. With the above as the main components, we finally develop our StepGuard, a new framework of Guarding Web Navigation via Single-Step Calibration. Experiments demonstrate that our approach significantly improves navigation and answer accuracy, setting new state-of-the-art performance on standard web navigation benchmarks.

</details>


### [179] [Structural Preservation and the Logical Expressiveness of Graph Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17882)
*Przemysław Andrzej Wałęga,Bernardo Cuenca Grau*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文从语义角度建立了图神经网络(GNN)与逻辑形式系统之间的桥梁，通过研究在嵌入、单射同态和同态等结构性质下保持不变的GNN分类器的逻辑表达能力，发现每一类GNN都对应一个分级模态逻辑的片段，并证明了这些类别的GNN都存在相应表达能力的架构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究通过固定架构选择（如聚合、组合和激活函数的类型）来建立GNN与逻辑形式系统之间的联系，但这些方法受限于具体的架构选择。本文希望从更抽象的语义角度出发，独立于具体架构选择来刻画GNN的逻辑表达能力。

Method: 采用语义视角，研究在嵌入、单射同态和同态三种结构性质下保序的GNN分类器类别。利用有界高度树的新良拟序（well-quasi-order）结果，得到展开不变类（unravelling-invariant classes）的有限表示。通过建立GNN与分级模态逻辑（graded modal logic）片段之间的对应关系来刻画表达能力。

Result: 证明了：(1) 在嵌入下保序的GNN类对应存在性分级模态逻辑；(2) 在单射同态下保序的GNN类对应存在性-正片段；(3) 在同态下保序的GNN类对应存在性-正模态逻辑。每一类GNN都存在具有相同表达能力的架构。

Conclusion: 本文从语义角度独立于具体架构选择刻画了GNN的逻辑表达能力，建立了GNN与分级模态逻辑之间的严格对应关系，为理解GNN的表达能力提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: Bridges between graph neural networks (GNNs) and logical formalisms have been established by fixing architectural choices, such as the types of aggregation, combination, and activation functions. These choices define restricted classes of GNNs for which tight correspondences with logical formalisms can be obtained, by showing that logical formulae can be translated into equivalent GNNs and, conversely, that GNNs can be translated into equivalent formulae.
  In this paper we take a semantic perspective by establishing the logical expressiveness of classes of GNN classifiers that are preserved under structural properties: embeddings (extensions), injective homomorphisms, and homomorphisms. We show that, for each such property, there exists a fragment of graded modal logic characterising the class of GNNs. In particular, preservation under embeddings, injective homomorphisms, and homomorphisms corresponds to existential graded modal logic, its existential-positive fragment, and existential-positive modal logic, respectively. These results characterise the expressiveness of broad classes of GNNs independently of specific architectural choices, but we also show that each of these classes admits a GNN architecture of the same expressiveness.
  Technically, our approach uses a new well-quasi-order result for trees of bounded height, yielding finite representations of unravelling-invariant classes.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning has extended from purely linguistic domains to multimodal scenarios; however, existing approaches often treat visual inputs as homogeneous or auxiliary signals, failing to capture the intricate and sample-specific dependencies between text and images in mathematical problem-solving. We first construct the MathVis-Fine dataset, augmenting fine-grained visual annotations with visual dependency ratings. Extensive experiments demonstrate that the MathVis-Fine framework effectively enhances visual perception progressively based on visual dependency, offering a more precise training framework for multimodal mathematical reasoning. We introduce DiagFlowBench, a dataset of 50 industrial diagnostic flowcharts from a consumer manufacturer converted into 1,676 multi-turn conversations that contrast compliant with out-of-scope utterances. ### [183] [PreAct: Computer-Using Agents that Get Faster on Repeated Tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17929)
*Bojie Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: PreAct 是一种让计算机操作代理通过将首次成功执行编译为状态机程序，后续直接重放而非重新推理，从而实现 8.5-13 倍加速的方法，并包含运行时校验和存储时验证机制确保可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的计算机操作代理每次执行任务都从零开始推理，即使是重复任务也需重新读取屏幕、重新推理每一步操作，导致大量计算浪费。作者希望让代理在重复执行已解决的任务时显著提速。

Method: PreAct 将首次成功执行编译为小型状态机程序（包含状态检查和动作转换），后续运行时直接重放该程序而非调用语言模型；每个步骤都会校验屏幕状态；新程序需通过独立评估器在干净状态下重新运行确认任务完成才能入库。

Result: 在移动、桌面和网页三种基准测试中实现 8.5-13 倍加速，无逐步骤的语言模型调用；存储时验证机制有效防止错误程序积累，带来每基准 1.75-2.6 个任务的提升；与强记录-重放基线持平；提示词、运行时护栏和程序检索方式影响不大。

Conclusion: PreAct 通过编译-重放范式有效提升重复任务的执行效率，同时通过状态校验和存储验证保证了可靠性，为计算机操作代理的实用化提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Computer-using agents drive real software through the screen -- clicking and typing -- but they solve every task from scratch: asked to repeat a task, an agent re-reads the screen, re-reasons every tap, and pays the full cost again. We present PreAct, which lets such an agent get faster on tasks it has done before. The first time it succeeds, PreAct compiles the run into a small state-machine program-states that check the screen, transitions that act-and on later runs replays it directly instead of invoking the agent 8.5-13x faster, with no per-step language-model calls. Replay is not blind: at each step PreAct checks that the screen matches what the program expects before acting, and hands control back to the agent the moment something is off.
  PreAct applies the same discipline when deciding what to keep: a freshly compiled program enters the store only if, re-run from a clean state, an independent evaluator confirms it solved the task-catching programs that replay to their last step yet leave the task undone. Across a mobile, a desktop, and a web benchmark, this store-time check separates repeated runs that improve from ones that degrade as faulty programs accumulate, worth 1.75-2.6 tasks per benchmark, the same direction on all three; a fallback that explores afresh when no program fits brings PreAct level with a strong record-and-replay baseline. We also report what did not matter: prompt wording, runtime guardrails, and whether a language model or a plain embedding retriever selects which program to reuse.

</details>


### [184] [How Inference Compute Shapes Frontier LLM Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17930)
*Jessica McFadyen,Ole Jorgensen,Harry Coppock,Kevin Wei,Cozmin Ududec*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了12个前沿语言模型在7个挑战性基准上的表现，发现更大的推理计算预算能显著提升性能，固定预算评估会低估模型真实能力，且不同基准对推理扩展方法的敏感度不同。作者建议评估应报告能力随推理计算的变化，明确协议选择，并在匹配预算下比较模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI评估往往在单一的、受限的计算预算下报告性能，导致低分可能反映的是评估设置而非模型真实能力。随着任务趋向更长的轨迹（工具使用、迭代求解），推理计算量对性能的影响日益显著，因此需要系统研究这一因素。

Method: 在7个挑战性基准（涵盖软件工程、数学、医学、网络安全）上评估12个前沿语言模型，采用三种简单的推理扩展干预：更大的token预算、上下文压缩、重复提交尝试（由模型自身或最小正确性反馈引导）。

Result: 1) 更大token预算在网络安全、FrontierMath、Humanity's Last Exam、TerminalBench等多个领域显著提升性能。2) 固定预算评估越来越低估前沿模型能力——新模型在大预算下解锁更难任务并更可靠解决。3) 不同基准对推理扩展方法的敏感度不同：重复提交普遍有效，但更大token预算、外部反馈和并行尝试的价值因基准而异。

Conclusion: 基准得分是协议依赖的。评估应报告能力随推理计算的变化函数，明确指定协议选择，并在共享的大计算范围内以匹配预算比较不同代际的模型，尤其是在安全或政策相关场景中。

Abstract: AI evaluations are shifting toward harder tasks that benefit from longer trajectories involving tool use and iterative problem solving. As a result, performance is increasingly sensitive to the amount and allocation of compute available at test time ("inference compute"). Yet many evaluations still report performance at a single restrictive budget, meaning that low scores may reflect the evaluation setup rather than the model's underlying capability. To test this, we evaluate up to 12 frontier language models on seven challenging benchmarks spanning software engineering, mathematics, medicine, and cybersecurity. We use a controlled setup combining three simple inference-scaling interventions: larger token budgets, context compaction, and repeated submission attempts, guided either by the model itself or by minimal correctness feedback. We find three main results. First, larger token budgets substantially improve performance on benchmarks across multiple domains, including cybersecurity, FrontierMath, Humanity's Last Exam, and TerminalBench. Second, fixed-budget evaluations can increasingly understate frontier capability as models advance. Newer models reach higher performance at large budgets, where they unlock harder tasks and solve them more reliably. Third, benchmarks differ in which inference-scaling methods help most: repeated submission broadly improves performance, but the value of larger token budgets, external feedback, and parallel attempts varies by benchmark. Overall, our results show that benchmark scores are protocol-dependent. We therefore argue that evaluations should report capability as a function of inference-time compute, specify protocol choices explicitly, and compare model generations over a large shared compute range at matched budgets, especially in safety- or policy-relevant settings.

### [185] [Small Initialization Matters for Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17945)
*Liangkai Hang,Junjie Yao,Zhiyu Li,Feiyu Xiong,Hongkang Yang,Zhi-Qin John Xu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大语言模型的进步通常归因于规模、数据和架构，但作者认为参数初始化是一个被忽视但类似基因的决定性因素，探索其对模型能力和训练轨迹的影响。

Method: 通过系统实验对比不同初始化尺度对预训练的影响，识别出两种限制小初始化优势的经验设置，并提出γ初始化规则——将初始化范围作为显式可调参数，默认使用小初始化。

Result: 缩小初始化范围一致提升预训练效果，在推理任务上增益最大；小初始化驱动参数先凝聚为低复杂度结构再扩展为丰富表征（"压缩即智能"）；增益集中在非平凡的上下文约束预测上。

Conclusion: 参数初始化是模型能力的关键决定因素，小初始化是一种几乎无成本的干预手段，能显著改善预训练并增强推理能力，建议将初始化范围作为显式超参数并默认使用小值。

Abstract: Large language models provide a tractable system for asking how intelligence itself emerges, rather than only how LLMs can be engineered. Although progress is usually attributed to scale, data and architecture, we show that parameter initialization is a gene-like determinant of training and, in particular, of model capacity. Reducing the initialization scale consistently improves pretraining, with the largest gains on reasoning-demanding tasks. We identify two widely used empirical settings that restrain the advantage of small initialization, and show how relaxing them restores favorable scaling. We further uncover a critical initialization that balances the reasoning and training. Mechanistically, small initialization drives a distinct developmental trajectory: parameters first condense into low-complexity structures and later expand into richer representations, giving concrete form to the idea that compression is intelligence. Token-level analyses show that the gains concentrate on non-trivial, context-constrained predictions rather than all tokens uniformly. These results motivate a simple $γ$-initialization rule: expose initialization rage as an explicit knob and use small initialization by default, an almost cost-free intervention that improves pretraining and strengthens reasoning across model scales.

### [187] [STAR: SpatioTemporal Adaptive Reward Allocation for Text-to-Image RL Post-Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17979)
*Jinjie Shen,Wei Deng,Xian Hu,Daiguo Zhou,Jian Luan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文提出STAR（时空自适应奖励分配）方法，用于文本到图像扩散/流模型的RL后训练。针对传统方法将奖励均匀分配给整个生成轨迹导致粒度不匹配的问题，STAR利用文本-图像注意力机制，根据图像区域与提示内容的相关性，动态地将组相对优势奖励分配到更相关的潜在区域，并对这些区域进行更强的策略更新。在Stable Diffusion 3.5 Medium上，STAR在GenEval（0.9759）、OCR文本渲染（0.9757）和PickScore（23.60）三项任务上均取得领先性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RL后训练方法将最终图像奖励转化为单一标量优势，并均匀作用于整个生成轨迹。但文本到图像生成具有时空结构：不同去噪步骤对应不同生成阶段，真正决定文本对齐的内容往往只出现在部分图像区域。这种粒度不匹配导致策略更新难以聚焦于实际影响奖励的生成组件。

Method: STAR利用生成模型内部的文本-图像注意力机制，从用户提示中真正关心的核心内容出发，构建随去噪步骤和时间步动态变化的空间分配图，将组相对优势奖励分配到更相关的潜在区域，并通过空间分辨的策略目标对这些区域施加更强的策略更新，且几乎不增加计算开销。

Result: 以Stable Diffusion 3.5 Medium为基础模型，在GenEval任务上达到0.9759，OCR文本渲染任务上达到0.9757，PickScore任务上达到23.60，均超越基线方法。

Conclusion: STAR通过时空自适应的奖励分配，在不改变外部奖励源的情况下，有效提升了组合语义对齐、文本渲染和偏好优化性能，解决了传统RL后训练中奖励分配粒度不匹配的问题。

Abstract: Existing RL post-training methods for text-to-image generation usually convert the final-image reward into a single scalar advantage and apply it with the same strength to the entire generative trajectory. However, text-to-image generation naturally has temporal and spatial structure: different denoising steps are responsible for different generation stages, and the content that truly determines text alignment often appears only in part of the image. This granularity mismatch makes it difficult for policy updates to focus on the generative components that actually affect the reward. To address this issue, we propose \textbf{SpatioTemporal Adaptive Reward (STAR) Allocation} for RL post-training of text-to-image diffusion and flow models. STAR uses text-image attention inside the generative model and starts from the core content that the user truly cares about in the prompt. It constructs spatial allocation maps that dynamically vary across denoising steps and rollouts, and allocates the same group-relative advantage to more relevant latent regions with almost no additional computational overhead. STAR then applies stronger policy updates to these regions through a spatially resolved policy objective. We use Stable Diffusion 3.5 Medium as the base model and evaluate on three tasks: GenEval, OCR text rendering, and PickScore. Experimental results show that STAR improves compositional semantic alignment, text rendering, and preference optimization without changing the external reward source, achieving $\mathbf{0.9759}$, $\mathbf{0.9757}$, and $\mathbf{23.60}$ on GenEval, OCR, and PickScore, respectively.

</details>


### [188] [LLM Consumer Behavior Theory: Foundations of a Novel Research Field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18005)
*Manon Reusens,Sofie Goethals,David Martens*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了"大语言模型消费者行为理论"这一新领域，研究在代理化市场中LLM作为自主决策者时的消费行为，从经济学和自然语言处理视角分析人类偏好如何被LLM代理反映和执行，并指出了理性假设、异质性等传统经济学假设在代理市场中可能失效的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM被越来越多地部署为替代用户做消费决策的自主代理，这一转变挑战了传统消费理论中"人类是主要决策者"的基本假设，因此需要建立新的理论框架来分析这种新型市场行为。

Method: 融合古典经济学、行为经济学以及自然语言处理的最新进展，对LLM决策、人类行为模拟和偏好获取等分散文献进行统一的经济学视角整合，识别代理化市场中理性假设和异质性假设可能失效的关键点。

Result: 提出了LLM消费行为理论的框架，明确了该领域的研究范畴，并识别出与对齐（alignment）、偏好表征（preference representation）和市场动态相关的开放性研究问题。本文为理论性论文，未提供实证验证。

Conclusion: 该论文为理解LLM作为消费者代理的经济行为提供了系统性理论框架，指出了传统经济学假设在AI代理市场中的局限性，并为未来关于偏好表征、对齐问题和市场动态研究指明了方向。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed as autonomous agents that make consumption decisions on behalf of users. This shift raises fundamental questions for consumer theory, which has traditionally modeled humans as the primary decision-makers. In this paper, we introduce LLM Consumer Behavior Theory, a new field of study concerned with analyzing consumer behavior in agentic markets. Drawing on classical and behavioral economics alongside recent advances in Natural Language Processing, we formalize how human preferences are reflected and acted upon by LLM-based agents, and how agent-level decisions aggregate into market demand. We unify previously fragmented literature on LLM decision-making, human behavior simulation, and preference elicitation under a common economic lens, highlighting where assumptions, such as rationality and heterogeneity, may fail in agentic markets. Rather than providing empirical validation, this paper outlines the scope of LLM consumer behavior and identifies open research questions related to alignment, preference representation, and market dynamics.

### [189] [PseudoBench: Measuring How Agentic Auto-Research Fuels Pseudoscience](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18060)
*Xinyang Liao,Lingyu Li,Huacan Liu,Tianle Gu,Yang Yao,Tong Zhu,Yan Teng,Yingchun Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 这篇论文提出了PseudoBench基准，用于评估AI科研代理识别和抵制伪科学的能力。测试7个顶尖AI系统发现，它们几乎不拒绝伪科学主张，甚至会包装得更具迷惑性，最高抵抗率仅27.4%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着基于大语言模型的代理进入自主科研领域，它们可能快速生成看似合理但具有误导性的研究，污染学术文献并侵蚀科学信任。因此，评估这些系统识别和抵制伪科学叙述的能力至关重要。

Method: 构建包含200个跨五个领域的伪科学声称-证据对的PseudoBench基准，通过端到端研究流程（从实验到论文撰写）评估AI代理。测试了7个最先进的AI代理系统。

Result: 当前AI系统几乎不拒绝伪科学前提（接近零拒绝率），最高抵抗率仅27.4%。更强的AI代理反而会将伪科学包装在更复杂的科学语言中，增加其表面可信度。

Conclusion: 当前AI系统存在助长伪科学的惊人能力，呼吁在广泛部署前进行科学对齐（scientific alignment）。

Abstract: As Large Language Model based agents enter autonomous scientific research, their ability to resist pseudoscience becomes increasingly important. Otherwise, such systems may rapidly generate plausible yet misleading studies that contaminate academic literature and erode trust in science. We present PseudoBench, an adversarial benchmark for evaluating whether agentic auto-research systems can identify and resist pseudoscientific narratives. PseudoBench contains 200 curated pseudoscientific claim-evidence pairs across five domains and evaluates agents through an end-to-end research pipeline from experiments to writing. Testing seven state-of-the-art agents, we find that current systems readily produce persuasive reports that align with pseudoscientific premises with near-zero refusal rates and the highest resistance of only 27.4%. Stronger agents risk packaging pseudoscience in more sophisticated scientific language, increasing its apparent credibility. These findings reveal an alarming capacity to fuel pseudoscience, calling for scientific alignment before widespread deployment.

### [190] [Agentic AI-based Framework for Mitigating Premature Diagnostic Handoff and Silent Hallucination in Healthcare Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18068)
*Divyansh Srivastava,Shreya Ghosh,Anshul Verma,Rajkumar Buyya*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一个多智能体框架，通过神经符号状态追踪门（确保OLDCARTS临床协议完整性）和认知不确定性量化门（计算语义熵拦截不确定输出）两种安全机制，解决LLM在医疗推理中的过早诊断移交和无声临床幻觉问题。在150个测试案例上，该框架将诊断精度从38.0%提升至49.3%（绝对提升11.3个百分点），并发现OLDCARTS完整性与语义熵之间存在显著负相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM和多智能体系统在医疗推理中虽展现出潜力，但开放式对话代理存在两个关键失败模式：过早进行诊断移交，以及可能在到达患者前未被检测到的无声临床幻觉。这两种缺陷严重威胁医疗安全，亟需有效的机制来约束和检测。

Method: 提出了一个多智能体框架，核心是用确定性编排约束替代"LLM作为裁判"的路由方式。包含两种安全机制：(1) 神经符号状态追踪门，强制要求OLDCARTS临床协议（发病、位置、持续时间、性质、加重/缓解因素、放射、时间、严重程度）的所有维度收集完整后才允许进行诊断；(2) 认知不确定性量化门，计算K=5个独立诊断样本间的语义熵（H），在传递前识别并拦截分歧较大的输出。

Result: 使用llama-3.1-70b-instruct模型驱动的模拟患者代理在150个测试案例上评估，完整架构达到49.3%的诊断精度，相比无约束基线绝对提升11.3个百分点。此外，观察到OLDCARTS完整性（σ）与语义熵（H）之间存在统计显著的负相关（r = -0.181, p < 0.05）。

Conclusion: 结构化信息收集（OLDCARTS协议的完整执行）能够降低诊断不确定性，该多智能体框架通过确定性约束和双重安全机制有效提升了医疗对话系统的安全性和诊断性能。

Abstract: Recent advances in Large Language Models (LLMs) and multi-agent systems have driven the rise of Agentic AI, showing promise for medical reasoning. However, open-ended conversational agents remain prone to two critical failure modes: premature diagnostic handoff and silent clinical hallucinations that may go undetected before reaching the patient. In this work, we propose a multi-agent framework that addresses both issues by replacing ``LLM-as-a-judge'' routing with deterministic orchestration constraints. The framework incorporates two safety mechanisms. First, a neuro-symbolic state-tracking gate enforces completeness of the OLDCARTS clinical protocol (Onset, Location, Duration, Character, Aggravating/Alleviating factors, Radiation, Timing, and Severity) by blocking diagnostic transitions until all required dimensions are collected. Second, an epistemic uncertainty quantification (UQ) gate computes semantic entropy (H) across K=5 independent diagnostic samples to identify and intercept divergent outputs before delivery.
  We evaluate the system using simulated patient agents powered by the llama-3.1-70b-instruct model on 150 test cases. The full architecture achieves 49.3% diagnostic precision, representing an absolute improvement of 11.3 percentage points over an unconstrained baseline. Additionally, we observe a statistically significant negative correlation (r = -0.181, p < 0.05) between OLDCARTS completeness (σ) and semantic entropy (H), suggesting that structured information gathering is associated with reduced diagnostic uncertainty.

### [191] [A Unified Framework for Context-Aware and Relation-Aware Graph Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18075)
*Haoyang Zhong,Yifei Sun,Antong Zhang,Chunping Wang,Lei Chen,Yang Yang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: HyGRAG提出了一种层次化图RAG框架，通过构建融合上下文和关系信息的摘要、在检索中利用这些综合表征实现涌现知识获取，并支持动态更新，在多跳推理任务上平均准确率提升9.7%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于图的RAG方法（实体中心型和块中心型）均锚定于原始文本，检索时仅进行相似性搜索，缺乏对知识的真正融合与涌现理解。

Method: 设计包含块节点和实体节点的混合图构建层次化索引结构，通过迭代聚类生成LLM摘要；设计上下文与关系感知的检索机制，跨抽象层级搜索并通过社区成员关系扩展；采用基于附加算法的动态知识更新，仅需局部重新摘要。

Result: 在多跳推理任务上平均准确率提升9.7%，且保持合理的效率。

Conclusion: HyGRAG通过层次化图结构和摘要融合，有效实现了跨文档的知识融合与涌现认知，在提升推理能力的同时支持动态更新，为RAG系统提供了新范式。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) has emerged as a paradigm for enhancing large language models (LLMs) with external knowledge, yet existing graph-based methods face a fundamental limitation: entity-centric and chunk-centric approaches operate on representations anchored to original text without true knowledge fusion. While entity-centric methods connect logically related content and chunk-centric methods preserve context, both retrieve information separately through similarity search, missing emergent understanding from their synthesis. In this paper, we propose HyGRAG, a hierarchical graph RAG framework that transcends source documents by addressing three core challenges: constructing summaries that genuinely integrate contextual and relational information, leveraging these synthesized representations to access emergent knowledge during retrieval, and efficiently updating hierarchical structures for dynamic corpora. Specifically, we design hierarchical index structures over hybrid graphs with both chunk and entity nodes, then iteratively cluster them and generate LLM-based summaries. Then, we design context and relation-aware retrieval that searches across all abstraction levels while expanding through community membership. Moreover, we enable dynamic knowledge update through attachment-based algorithms with only local re-summarization. Experimental results show that HyGRAG improves the average accuracy of multi-hop reasoning tasks by 9.7%, while maintaining reasonable efficiency.

In this paper, we improve upon IsabeLLM, the automated theorem proving tool in Isabelle. ### [193] [Trust the Right Teacher: Quality-Aware Self-Distillation for GUI Grounding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18101)
*Jingyuan Huang,Zuming Huang,Yucheng Shi,Tianze Yang,Xiaoming Zhai,Wei Chu,Ninghao Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出质量感知自蒸馏方法，通过软正确性门控和教师概率缩放改善GUI接地任务中坐标令牌的教师信号质量，在多个基准测试上取得一致性提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在GUI接地任务中，现有的on-policy自蒸馏方法(OPSD)在学生生成的前缀偏离目标坐标时，教师提供的坐标令牌信号质量会下降，导致不可靠的监督信号。

Method: 提出质量感知自蒸馏(QASD)，包含两个互补组件：1)软正确性感知门控，检查教师在当前学生生成前缀下能否完成目标框，对不能完成的信号降权；2)教师概率缩放，用教师置信度作为轻量因子校准门控后监督的强度。

Result: 在六个GUI接地基准测试上，该方法一致性地提升了基础模型性能，并优于强基线方法。且实验表明两个组件缺一不可，单独使用均无法提升整体性能。

Conclusion: 软正确性门控和教师概率缩放两个机制发挥互补作用：门控抑制不可靠的坐标令牌监督，概率缩放校准剩余信号的强度，两者结合才能有效提升GUI接地性能。

Abstract: Graphical user interface (GUI) grounding requires vision-language models (VLMs) to identify small target elements in high-resolution screenshots and predict precise screen coordinates. On-policy self-distillation (OPSD) is a promising post-training approach for this coordinate-sensitive task, since it provides dense token-level teacher signals beyond hard coordinate labels. However, naive OPSD is not well suited to GUI grounding: OPSD evaluates the teacher on student-generated prefixes, the quality of coordinate-token teacher signals can degrade when the prefix has already deviated from the target coordinate, leading to unreliable teacher signal. To mitigate this, We propose quality-aware self-distillation for VLM-based GUI grounding, which improves coordinate-token teacher-signal quality through soft correctness-aware gating and teacher-probability scaling. The soft correctness-aware gate checks whether the teacher's current coordinate-token prediction can still be completed into the ground-truth box under the student-generated prefix. If not, the corresponding teacher signal is down-weighted. Teacher-probability scaling then uses the teacher's confidence as a lightweight factor to further calibrate the strength of the gated supervision. A key empirical finding is that neither component alone improves overall performance, whereas combining them consistently improves performance. This suggests that the two mechanisms play complementary roles: correctness-aware gating suppresses unreliable coordinate-token supervision, while teacher-probability scaling calibrates the strength of the remaining signals. Experiments across six GUI grounding benchmarks show that our method consistently improves the base model and outperforms strong baselines.

### [195] [Knowledge Reutilization in Meta-Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18132)
*Yuan Meng,Bo Wang,Juan de los Rios Ruiz,Xiangtong Yao,Zhenshan Bing,Fuchun Sun,Alois Knoll*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出一种元知识复用框架，通过在动力学简化智能体上学习任务知识，经语义-幅度接口和时序适配器迁移到异构智能体，显著降低追踪误差并提高样本效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有端到端元强化学习方法将任务推理与具体智能体的控制耦合，导致任务语义不清晰、样本效率低且无法跨智能体重用。

Method: 1) 在动力学简化智能体上学习元知识；2) 贝叶斯非参数先验组织潜在任务模式；3) 高层策略生成任务级幅度引导；4) 语义-幅度接口+轻量时序适配器将冻结元知识转化为时序对齐的子目标。

Result: 在多个运动智能体上，最终步跟踪误差降低94.75%-99.79%，仅用约23.8%的交互数据即可达到可比部署性能。

Conclusion: 解耦任务推理与具体控制是提升跨智能体元学习效率和泛化性的有效路径。

Abstract: Meta-reinforcement learning enables fast adaptation by extracting shared structure from related tasks, but existing end-to-end methods often couple task inference with embodiment-specific control. This coupling can obscure non-parametric task semantics, reduce sample efficiency, and limit cross-agent reuse. We propose a meta-knowledge reutilization framework that learns task-level knowledge on a dynamics-simplified agent and transfers it to heterogeneous agents. The framework uses a Bayesian non-parametric prior to organize latent task modes and a high-level policy to generate task-level magnitude guidance. To bridge reusable task knowledge with different embodiments, we introduce a semantic-magnitude interface and a lightweight temporal adaptor, which convert frozen meta-knowledge into temporally aligned subgoals for embodiment-specific low-level controllers. Experiments on multiple locomotion agents show that our framework reduces final-step tracking error by 94.75% -- 99.79% compared with recent state-of-the-art baselines and achieves comparable deployment performance with about 23.8% of their interaction data.

</details>


### [196] [Your AI Travel Agent Would Book You a Bullfight: An Agentic Benchmark for Implicit Animal Welfare in Frontier AI Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18142)
*Jasmine Brazilek,Oliver Tulio,Joel Christoph,Miles Tidmarsh,Carol Kline,Arturs Kanepajs*

Result: 所有模型得分低于随机水平64%，最佳为Claude Opus 4.7（53%）。福利提示在大模型上提升显著（Claude和GPT-5.5提升47-63个百分点），在DeepSeek和Gemini上提升有限（<12个百分点）。审计未发现模型识别出评估意图的证据。

Conclusion: 当前AI智能体在代理任务中普遍无法避免动物剥削选项，文本回复的福利推理不能直接迁移到工具使用场景。需要针对智能体部署设计专门的评估和干预机制，并考虑跨文化领域的类别差异。

Abstract: AI agents are moving from advisors to actors, booking travel, planning menus, and running procurement on behalf of users. Existing benchmarks for AI and animal welfare evaluate model text responses to question-answer prompts, leaving open whether the welfare reasoning surfaced in those responses transfers to agentic deployment where the model must take actions with tools. We introduce TAC (Travel Agent Compassion), the first agentic benchmark measuring whether AI agents avoid options involving animal exploitation when acting on behalf of users. TAC presents an AI agent with twelve hand-authored travel booking scenarios across six categories of animal exploitation, augmented to forty-eight samples to control for price, rating, and position confounds. We evaluate seven frontier models from four labs. Every model scores below the chance level of sixty-four percent, with the best performer (Claude Opus 4.7) at fifty-three percent. A single welfare-aware sentence in the system prompt yields gains of forty-seven to sixty-three percentage points in Claude and GPT-5.5, twenty-six points in GPT-5.2, and under twelve points in DeepSeek and Gemini. An auxiliary Inspect Scout audit of 288 base-condition transcripts from the top two performers, using Gemini 2.5 Flash Lite as judge, flags zero transcripts for evaluation awareness, suggesting the below-chance rates do not stem from the models recognising the evaluation. We discuss implications for category-level variation across cultural domains, the limits of text-response welfare benchmarks, and the EU General-Purpose AI Code of Practice systemic risk framework.

### [197] [Memory as a Wasting Asset: Pricing Flash Endurance for Embodied Agents, and the Limits of Doing So](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18144)
*Josef Liyanjun Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出将机器人闪存耐久性视为折旧资本，通过单一影子价格η构建磨损增强的每字节索引，实现RAM/板载NVM/云三级存储的成本最优分配。实证发现价值-写入关联χ的符号随部署场景变化（正/零/负），仅在χ>0时最优策略呈非单调性——最有价值记忆被移出闪存。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器人存储系统未考虑闪存擦写次数（~几千次）作为不可再生资源的成本，导致存储分配非最优。

Method: 将耐久性视为折旧资本，定义影子价格η构建磨损增强的每字节索引，在RAM/NVM/云三级层次结构中进行成本最小化存储分配。通过真实机器人日志测量价值-写入关联χ。

Result: χ符号取决于部署场景：重复长时操作χ≈+1.0×10⁻³（正），短时操作χ≈0，非重复遥操作χ为负。耐久性预算仅在低端QLC/eMMC（~1000 P/E）上有约束力，高端TLC（3000 P/E）上不活跃。

Conclusion: 磨损感知放置是否能提升任务价值仍待验证——χ基于价值代理测量，非单调最优虽经证明但尚未在数据中观测到。

Abstract: A robot's flash endurance is a non-renewable stock: every persisted write spends one of a few thousand program/erase cycles and never refills, yet no fielded robot memory system prices which memories are worth an erase cycle. We treat embodied memory as depreciating capital and price that stock with a single endurance shadow price $η$, which makes cost-minimizing placement across a RAM / on-board NVM / cloud hierarchy a threshold in a wear-augmented per-byte index. The index is cost-optimal whatever the sign of the value-write association $χ$; only when $χ> 0$ does the optimum turn non-monotone, sending a robot's most valuable memories off its flash.
  The pivot is thus empirical, and we measure $χ$ on real robot logs at a pre-specified gate: its sign is a property of the deployment regime -- positive on recurrent long-horizon manipulation ($\hatχ \approx +1.0 \times 10^{-3}$, replicated at full power), null on a shorter-horizon suite, and negative on non-recurrent teleoperation. Two boundaries scope the result. The endurance budget is dormant on premium 3,000-P/E TLC at datasheet prices and binding on the commodity QLC/eMMC ($\sim$1,000 P/E) that cheaper edge robots run. And where it binds, a learned wear-aware controller only ties price-based routing on task value, because realized value is tier-invariant across RAM, NVM, and cloud: the rent governs device lifetime and cost, not task performance. Whether wear-aware placement improves task value remains open -- $χ$ is measured against a value proxy, and the non-monotone optimum, while proven, is not yet observed in data.

</details>

To address these challenges, we propose WEQA, a query-adaptive agent framework that unifies LLM reasoning with specialized wearable analytical and modeling tools. An LLM controller is employed to synthesize execution plans and dynamically route each query to the appropriate combination of sensor analysis and pretrained models, and perform grounded response auditing with external knowledge. We also curate a benchmark spanning four open wearable datasets comprising analytic and predictive tasks in three different health domains. Experiments show that our framework is 24% more accurate than LLM and agentic baselines, and a blinded study with 12 medical experts and 8 users shows substantial gains in usefulness and clinical soundness.

In this paper, we propose a self-evolving ZS-OGN framework that enables continuous test-time improvement. Then, we propose a retrieval strategy based on upper confidence bound, selecting effective rules by balancing semantic relevance and historical success. ### [203] [Intermittent Strategic Cooperation of Two Selfish Agents on Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17216)
*Itay Shedlezki,Noa Agmon*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 研究两个自利智能体在时空约束下的间歇性战略合作路径规划问题，证明纯纳什均衡的存在性，提出多项式时间枚举算法，并基于博弈论分析合作稳定性与协调机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 两个自利智能体在路径规划中虽然可以通过合作互惠，但合作具有战略脆弱性，智能体可能在路径任意点偏离合作。需要系统分析何时以及如何实现稳定的合作。

Method: 将问题建模为双人博弈，刻画纯纳什均衡（PNE）联合策略的结构特征；证明每个IC2PP实例至少存在一个PNE；设计多项式时间算法枚举所有相关PNE；采用议价理论选择概念作为多均衡下的协调机制。

Result: 证明了稳定合作必须遵循高度受限的形式；每个实例至少存在一个PNE；提出了多项式时间枚举算法；通过实验比较了不同均衡下的个体旅行时间和社会福利。

Conclusion: IC2PP中的合作虽然可行，但结构受限；存在多个均衡时可通过议价理论机制实现协调；为自利智能体间的间歇性合作路径规划提供了理论基础和计算工具。

Abstract: We study strategic space- and time-constrained cooperation between two self-interested agents through the Intermittent Strategic Cooperation-Based Two-Agent Path Planning (IC2PP) problem, a shortest-path game on graphs in which agents navigate toward individual targets while optionally cooperating at specific nodes to reduce their own travel times. Although such cooperation can strictly benefit both agents, it is strategically fragile: agents may deviate at any point along their paths. Modeled as a 2-player game, we characterize the structure of Pure Nash Equilibrium (PNE) joint strategies in IC2PP, and show that stable cooperation must follow a highly constrained form. We further prove that at least one PNE exists in every instance of IC2PP, and present a polynomial-time algorithm for enumerating all relevant PNEs. When multiple equilibria arise, we study coordination mechanisms based on bargaining-theoretic selection concepts and empirically compare equilibrium outcomes in terms of individual travel times and social welfare.

### [204] [Trustworthy Self-Composable Big-Data-as-a-Service: An LLM-Orchestrated Multi-Agent Framework for Automated Data Engineering, AutoML, MLOps Deployment, and Drift-Aware Lifecycle Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17915)
*Aueaphum Aueawatthanaphisut,Badri Raj Lamichhane*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于LLM编排的多智能体协作框架，用于实现可信赖、可自组合的大数据即服务（BDaaS）全生命周期自动化，涵盖数据摄取、清洗、特征工程、AutoML训练、模型评估、MLOps部署、监控和漂移检测，并通过原型实验验证了其在生命周期可靠性方面的优势。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将BDaaS生命周期分解为多个专用智能体（数据摄取、清洗、特征工程、AutoML训练、模型评估、MLOps部署、监控、漂移检测），由中央LLM编排层协调执行、验证中间输出、管理工作流上下文并支持动态工作流组合，同时集成了共享工件治理、可复现性支持、人在环路检查点和漂移感知反馈循环。

Result: 在包含缺失值、分类变量、异常值、类别不平衡和模拟协变量漂移的基准表格数据集上，该多智能体BDaaS管道在预测性能上与基线方法相当，同时在生命周期级可靠性（工作流完成率、工件可追溯性、部署就绪性、可复现性和漂移恢复）方面表现更优。

Conclusion: LLM编排的多智能体系统能够将传统AutoML扩展到可信赖、自适应且面向生产的BDaaS生命周期自动化。

Abstract: Big-Data-as-a-Service (BDaaS) platforms require re liable automation across data ingestion, cleaning, feature engi neering, model development, deployment, and post-deployment monitoring. However, existing LLM-based data science agents and AutoML systems mainly focus on isolated workflow stages, leaving limited support for lifecycle-level orchestration, artifact governance, human oversight, and drift-aware adaptation. This paper proposes a trustworthy self-composable BDaaS frame work based on LLM-orchestrated multi-agent collaboration. The proposed architecture decomposes the BDaaS lifecycle into specialized agents for data ingestion, data cleaning, feature engineering, AutoML training, model evaluation, MLOps de ployment, monitoring, and drift detection. A central LLM or chestration layer coordinates agent execution, validates interme diate outputs, manages workflow context, and enables dynamic workflow composition. The framework also incorporates shared artifact governance, reproducibility support, human-in-the-loop checkpoints, and drift-aware feedback loops. A prototype-based evaluation is conducted using controlled tabular benchmark datasets with missing values, categorical variables, outliers, class imbalance, and simulated covariate drift. Compared with manual ML, AutoML-only, and single-agent LLM baselines, the pro posed multi-agent BDaaS pipeline achieves competitive predictive performance while improving lifecycle-level reliability, including workflow completion, artifact traceability, deployment readiness, reproducibility, and drift recovery. The results suggest that LLM-orchestrated multi-agent systems can extend conventional AutoML toward trustworthy, adaptive, and production-oriented BDaaS lifecycle automation.

</details>

Lyapunov analysis yields the stabilization condition lambda > alpha/Cm. We construct the ADE (Agent Delivery Engineering) four-layer framework (L1 Physical Laws through L4 User Adaptation) with 23 core components. Validation spans 100K-scale experiments and 33.6 days of production monitoring. ### [207] [On the Reliability of Networks of AI Agents: Density Evolution, Stopping Sets, and Architecture Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18121)
*Ehsan Aghazadeh,Hossein Pishro-Nik*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出一种用稀疏因子图（类似LDPC码）建模多智能体协作系统的方法，将任务分解为二元子声明，使用布尔验证节点，分析三种擦除失效模式（弃权、无输出、消息丢失），并推广密度进化理论来预测系统性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代AI系统常由多个不完美智能体协作完成任务，但其成功原因和失败条件尚不清晰，缺乏理论分析框架。

Method: 将多智能体系统建模为稀疏角色类型因子图，节点为布尔验证器，消息传递采用逻辑强制规则（支持XOR、AND、OR、蕴涵、Horn约束），并推广编码理论中的密度进化方法。

Result: 证明了密度进化定理，可预测随机角色类型架构上未解决子声明的渐近比例；XOR情况恢复经典LDPC递归；AND情况揭示正负验证证书的不对称性。

Conclusion: 该理论框架能够分析三种不同擦除失效模式的传播，且非线性验证函数和值不对称性使得问题不能简化为单一有效信道，需要新的阈值、有限长和逆界结果。

Abstract: Modern AI systems increasingly solve a task not with a single model call but with several imperfect agents working together: some propose pieces of a solution, others verify them, and the results are combined. These systems often outperform any single model, yet it is rarely clear why they succeed or when they will fail. We model such a system as message passing on a sparse graph, the structure that underlies low-density parity-check (LDPC) codes, and extend the density-evolution machinery of coding theory to this richer setting. In our model a task is a set of coupled binary subclaims, and an agent architecture is a sparse, role-typed factor graph whose check nodes are noisy Boolean verifier nodes, each computing a local Boolean function of the subclaims it touches. Three distinct failure modes, all modeled as erasures (an agent abstaining, a verifier returning no usable output, and a message lost between two agents), propagate as the agents exchange set-valued messages. The check agents combine these messages by a single logical-forcing rule that specializes to XOR, AND, OR, implication, and Horn constraints. This is more than a relabeling of LDPC theory: the verifier functions are nonlinear and value-asymmetric, and the three failure modes do not reduce to a single effective channel, so they require new threshold, finite-length, and converse results rather than a direct reuse of parity-check density evolution. We prove a density-evolution theorem that predicts the asymptotic fraction of unresolved subclaims on random role-typed architectures, with an extension to deterministic, locally tree-like graph sequences. The XOR case recovers the classical LDPC recursion on the binary erasure channel (BEC); the AND case exposes an asymmetry between positive and negative verifier certificates.

### [208] [Correct When Paired, Wrong When Split: Decoupling and Editing Modality-Specific Neurons in MLLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17057)
*Tingchao Fu,Wenkai Wang,Fanxiao Li,Huadong Zhang,Jinhong Zhang,Dayang Li,Yunyun Dong,Renyang Liu,Wei Zhou*

TL;DR: 论文发现多模态大模型的知识编辑存在“编辑解耦失败”问题：多模态输入下知识可更新，但单模态输入下仍回退旧知识。提出DECODE方法，通过解耦和定位模态特异性神经元组来统一更新知识，实验证明有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出DECODE方法，显式解耦并定位模态特异性的神经元组，对目标知识进行针对性更新，使知识编辑在不同模态触发条件下都能有效传播。

Result: 大量实验表明，DECODE在多模态和单模态触发条件下均能一致地实现有效的知识更新，缓解了编辑解耦失败问题。

Conclusion: 多模态大模型的实体知识不是统一存储的，而是分布在解耦的模态特异性通路中；DECODE通过解耦定位模态特异性神经元组，弥合了多模态与单模态间的知识更新差距。

Abstract: Although Knowledge Editing provides an efficient mechanism for updating the knowledge of Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs), we find that current paradigms still suffer from an important yet remain underexplored issue : editing decoupling failure, where entity-related knowledge can be updated when the model is triggered by multimodal inputs (text--image query pairs), however, it often reverts to outdated pre-edit facts when the paired inputs are split into unimodal ones. Our in-depth empirical analysis reveals that the entity knowledge in MLLMs is not stored as a unified representation, but is instead distributed across disentangled modality-specific pathways. As a result, updates biased toward multimodal queries fail to propagate effectively to unimodal circuits. To bridge this gap, we propose DECODE, which explicitly disentangles and localizes modality-specific neuron groups for targeted knowledge. Extensive experiments demonstrate that DECODE consistently achieves effective knowledge updates under different modality triggers, thereby mitigating editing decoupling failures.

### [209] [Diagnosing and Repairing Shape-Prior Shortcuts in Long-Range Single-Shot Fringe Projection Profilometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17093)
*Adam Haroon,Anush Lakshman,Cody Fleming,Beiwen Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对远距离（1.5-2.1米）单次条纹投影轮廓术（FPP）中的物理退化问题，利用机械可解释性（MI）和共形不确定性量化（UQ）诊断出基线UNet依赖物体边界形状先验而非条纹相位解码的失败机制，提出PhiCalNet通过架构修复（输出包裹相位+可微标定层）将物体MAE降低3.3倍至4.46 mm，MI与UQ在故障定位上达成一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于学习的单次FPP主要研究近距离场景，远距离（>1 m）存在三个未解决问题：强度平方反比衰减导致条纹信噪比降低、物理真值退化；单次图像缺乏条纹阶次信息导致病态；且缺乏对架构的机制性研究。

Method: 采用"诊断-修复-验证"框架：（1）使用线性探针、Grad-CAM、平面分布外测试三种探针诊断基线UNet失败原因为依赖边界形状先验；（2）提出PhiCalNet，架构上输出包裹相位而非深度，并添加固定可微标定层实现相位到深度的映射，从假设空间中移除形状先验解；（3）使用物理信息损失函数进行消融验证；（4）采用共形UQ进行像素级不确定性量化验证诊断结果。

Result: 在包含15,600张条纹图像、50个物体的真实感合成基准（1.5-2.1 m）上：基线UNet物体MAE为14.54 mm；PhiCalNet将MAE降低3.3倍至4.46 mm，残差仅来自±π包裹不连续处的0.103%像素；剔除前5%高不确定性像素后PhiCalNet RMSE降低64%（20.6→7.4 mm），而基线仅降低3.5%。

Conclusion: MI与UQ在故障定位上收敛一致，验证了架构修复的有效性；物理信息损失对深度回归网络无增益，隔离出架构为关键因素；共形UQ确认了诊断结果，表明该方法在远距离FPP中具有显著优势。

Abstract: Learning-based single-shot fringe projection profilometry (FPP) has been studied mostly at close range. The long-range regime (standoff beyond 1 m) remains largely unaddressed: inverse-square intensity falloff lowers fringe signal-to-noise ratio and degrades physical ground truth, the single-shot problem is ill-posed because fringe-order information is absent from one image, and these architectures have not been studied mechanistically. We present a diagnose-repair-verify study using mechanistic interpretability (MI) and conformal uncertainty quantification (UQ) as convergent diagnostics: they agree on one physical failure locus, driving and verifying an architectural repair. On a photorealistic synthetic benchmark (15,600 fringe images, 50 objects at 1.5-2.1 m), a best UNet baseline reaches 14.54 mm object mean absolute error (MAE). Three probes (linear probing, Grad-CAM, flat-plane out-of-distribution test) converge: the baseline solves the task via object-boundary shape priors rather than fringe-phase decoding. We repair this with PhiCalNet, which outputs wrapped phase rather than depth and applies a fixed differentiable calibration layer mapping phase to depth, removing the shape-prior solution from the hypothesis space architecturally rather than by a loss penalty. A physics-informed loss that enforces the same physics as a soft penalty on a depth-regressing network yields no measurable gain, isolating the architecture as the operative factor. PhiCalNet reduces object MAE 3.3x to 4.46 mm; the residual is carried by 0.103% of pixels at the +/-pi wrap discontinuity. Pixel-wise conformal UQ confirms the diagnosis: rejecting the top 5% of object pixels by snapshot disagreement cuts PhiCalNet RMSE by 64% (20.6->7.4 mm) versus 3.5% for the baseline. MI and UQ converge on the same failure locus.

</details>


### [210] [Informative Missingness to Generate Irregular Clinical Time Series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17106)
*Hadi Mehdizavareh,Gabriele Santangelo,Giovanna Nicora,Simon Lebech Cichosz,Arianna Dagliati,Arijit Khan,Riccardo Bellazzi*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于TimeDiff框架扩展，将图表时间对齐到4小时间隔，将入院记录分割为7天窗口，生成每个实验室值与对应观察指示变量配对的时间序列。通过互补扩散目标联合学习连续实验室值和离散缺失模式，并应用标准变换和归一化稳定训练。

Conclusion: 该扩散模型可作为开发临床基础模型的初始组件，生成的合成先验保留了关键的生理-缺失关系，为后续训练Prior-Data Fitted Networks（利用信息缺失）奠定基础，扩展工作将对此进行进一步研究。

Abstract: Laboratory tests in electronic health records are collected irregularly, and the absence of a test order can be as informative as the measurement itself. Such missingness reflects clinicians' decisions and patient physiology, making it important to model it directly rather than treat it as a preprocessing artifact. Here we present a diffusion-based approach for generating clinical time series that jointly models laboratory values and their observation patterns using the public Data Analytics Challenge on Missing Data Imputation (DACMI) benchmark derived from MIMIC-III. To preserve realistic sampling, we align chart times into 4-hour intervals and segment admissions into 7-day windows, producing trajectories that pair each lab value with a corresponding observation indicator. Standard transformations and normalization are applied to stabilize training. Our method extends the TimeDiff framework to learn continuous lab values and discrete missingness patterns through complementary diffusion objectives. Experiments show that the generated data closely match real patient trajectories across individual lab distributions and joint value-missingness embeddings, demonstrating that diffusion models can capture clinically meaningful dependencies between patient physiology and clinicians' testing behavior under MNAR-like (missing-not-at-random) missingness. These preliminary results indicate that our model can serve as an initial component toward developing clinical foundation models. By producing synthetic priors that preserve key physiology-missingness relationships, this work motivates the subsequent training of Prior-Data Fitted Networks capable of leveraging informative missingness, which we will investigate in the extended work.

### [211] [Models Take Notes at Prefill: KV Cache Can Be Editable and Composable](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17107)
*Bojie Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文发现前缀缓存中，KV缓存的重用主要由下游"笔记"（结论性表示）驱动，而非字段本身的KV向量。基于此，提出可编辑（通过勘误修正）和可组合（位置无关拼接）两种能力，实现与全量重计算决策一致但延迟最高降低14.9倍的推理方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有前缀缓存要求共享前缀完全一致，字段改动即导致整个下游缓存失效。作者试图探究字段KV向量对模型决策的真实贡献度，以实现更灵活的缓存机制。

Method: 通过因果分析跨四个模型家族，发现预填充阶段模型已将字段决定的结论写入下游"笔记"表示，而字段自身的KV向量对决策贡献不足1%。基于此提出：(1) 可编辑性：通过勘误（erratum）修改笔记，结合思维链（CoT）可仅编辑字段恢复决策；(2) 可组合性：利用笔记的位置无关性，将预编译技能经RoPE重定位后拼接到任意上下文，实现O(L)而非O(L^2)的首令牌延迟。

Result: 编辑字段+CoT可在8B模型上恢复1.00决策，仅需约1%计算量；组合策略在十二个模型上达到logit余弦相似度0.90-0.999；统一编辑+组合代理与全量重计算决策一致，延迟降低最高14.9倍；在vLLM在线基准测试中保持98.5%前缀缓存命中率，p90首令牌延迟降低53-398倍。

Conclusion: 将KV缓存重新理解为"备忘录化的笔记"（memoized conclusions），证明其可编辑和可组合特性。该方法适用于任意逐token注意力KV缓存，跨尺度、量化、MoE、多模态等场景有效，并通过小型适配器扩展到多种注意力变体。由于勘误机制是追加式的，可与生产级前缀缓存无缝兼容。

Abstract: Prefix caching reuses prefill only across an exactly shared prefix, so one changed field invalidates the entire downstream cache. Yet overwriting the field's own key/value vectors and reusing the rest leaves the model acting on the old value. The reason, established causally across four model families: at prefill the model has already written the field-conditioned conclusion onto downstream notes; the field's own key/value drives under 1% of the decision. Read as a notebook of memoized conclusions, two capabilities follow. (1) It is editable. A salient erratum amends the notes; and with chain-of-thought, editing the field alone recovers the decision (1.00 at 8B, ~1% compute), while without CoT it is ignored. (2) It is composable. The notes are position-portable, so a precompiled skill can be RoPE-repositioned and spliced into any context, indistinguishable from full recompute (logit cosine 0.90-0.999, twelve models) at O(L) rather than O(L^2) time-to-first-token. A unified edit+compose agent stays decision-identical to recompute at up to 14.9x lower latency. The approach applies to any per-token attention KV cache, validated across scale, quantization, Mixture-of-Experts, and multimodal caches, and extends to several attention variants through small adapters. Because the erratum is append-only, it composes with production prefix caching: in an online vLLM benchmark it keeps the prefix cache-aligned (98.5% hit-rate), cutting p90 time-to-first-token by 53-398x.

</details>


### [212] [Verified Detection and Prevention of Concurrency Anomalies in Multi-Agent Large Language Model Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17182)
*Sajjad Khan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文对多智能体LLM系统的并发异常进行了形式化建模和验证，提出了从L0到L4的一致性层次结构，并在Rust运行时中实现了这些层次。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体LLM系统通过内存存储、向量索引和工具注册表共享状态，但现有运行时缺乏对并发异常的系统性理解和形式化保证。

Method: 使用TLA+形式化定义了四种并发异常（stale-generation, phantom-tool, causal-cascade, tool-effect reordering），构建了L0-L4一致性层次，通过274个Verus验证义务证明检测器的正确性，并在三个Rust运行时中实现。

Result: 实现了从L0到L2的部署运行（L2跨三个模型家族120次回话验证）；发现了ByteDance的deer-flow中的静默丢失更新并形式化修复；发现了LangGraph中ToolNode的工具效应重排序问题并通过L3提交顺序排序器解决。

Conclusion: 本文贡献在于经过机器验证的检测器、精化和可实现性工件，而非异常现象本身；证明了多智能体LLM运行时中一致性层次的可实现性和严格分离。

Abstract: Multi-agent LLM systems share state through memory stores, vector indices, and tool registries. We model such sharing as long-running read-generate-write operations under deterministic-generation semantics -- the regime durable-execution engines enforce by deterministic replay -- and formalize four concurrency anomalies in TLA+: stale-generation, phantom-tool, causal-cascade, and tool-effect reordering, structural analogues of classical isolation anomalies, each with a TLC counter-example. The exclusion lattice over these anomalies is trivial; the contribution is the mechanically verified realizability and strict separation of one maximal chain within it, $L_0 \subsetneq \cdots \subsetneq L_4$, to our knowledge the first machine-checked consistency hierarchy for such runtimes. A development of 274 Verus obligations (zero assume, zero admit; trust base: two structural axioms and a mutex correspondence) proves the detectors sound and complete against the specifications and each runtime its avoidance set. Three deployed Rust runtimes realize L0-L1 (pessimistic locking, serializable snapshot isolation, default-SI), each verified against stale-generation and refined to its state machine; L2-L4 are exec-mode-verified with dependency-free prevention twins (A3, A6, A2: 0/1000 versus 1000/1000), and L2 is run live across three model families (A3 prevented in all 120 retracted sessions). We reproduce a silent lost update in ByteDance's deer-flow, formalizing its fix as a verified $L_0 \to L_1$ refinement, and exhibit tool-effect reordering in LangGraph's ToolNode on unmodified output, removed by an L3 commit-order sequencer. The verified detector, refinements, and realizability artifacts are the contribution; the phenomena and lattice are classical.

</details>

These results show that domain-specific pre-training provides a clear advantage over simpler baselines and larger LLMs. Investing in manageable, domain-aware models is more effective for computational pharmacovigilance than simply scaling model size.

### [215] [MODE: Modality-Decomposed Expert-Level Mixed-Precision Quantization for MoE Multimodal LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17118)
*Yuanteng Chen,Peisong Wang,Zhilei Liu,Nanxin Zeng,Yuantian Shao,Shiqiang Lang,Tao Liu,Chuangyi Li,Qinghao Hu,Gang Li,Jing Liu,Jian Cheng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出MODE框架，通过解耦模态、过滤冗余视觉token及整数线性规划，解决MoE-MLLM混合精度量化中专家重要性估计的跨模态和模态内偏差问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MoE-MLLM虽然性能优异但GPU显存过高，需要压缩。现有专家级混合精度量化方法在MoE-MLLM上效果不佳，因为存在两种被忽视的偏差：跨模态层面视觉token数量占优导致专家选择频率偏向视觉，忽视了对文本模态重要的专家；视觉内部层面大量冗余token进一步扭曲频率统计，掩盖了对信息性视觉内容重要的专家。

Method: 提出MODE框架：(1) 按模态分解专家选择频率；(2) 过滤冗余视觉token获得去噪后的视觉频率；(3) 评估每个模态的量化敏感性作为频率估计的补充信号；(4) 将这些信号整合到整数线性规划(ILP)中，在给定预算下为每个专家分配位宽。

Result: 在W3A16设置下平均性能损失限制在2.9%以内，在极端2-bit设置下增益更大。

Conclusion: MODE框架特别适合MoE-MLLM，能有效缓解跨模态和模态内偏差，在压缩比和性能之间取得良好平衡。

Abstract: Mixture-of-Experts Multimodal Large Language Models (MoE-MLLMs) offer remarkable performance but incur prohibitive GPU memory costs, making compression essential. Among PTQ methods, expert-level mixed-precision quantization has proven effective for MoE-LLMs, yet suffers notable degradation on MoE-MLLMs due to two overlooked biases in expert importance estimation. (1) At the cross-modal level, the numerical dominance of vision tokens causes expert selection frequency to be dominated by vision tokens, masking experts that are critical to the text modality; (2) at the intra-vision level, the large proportion of redundant vision tokens further skew frequency statistics, obscuring experts critical for informative visual content. To bridge gaps, we propose MODE, a modality-decomposed expert-level mixed-precision quantization framework for MoE-MLLMs that decomposes expert selection frequency by modality, filters redundant vision tokens to obtain denoised visual frequency, and further evaluates quantization sensitivity per modality as a complementary signal to frequency-based estimation. These signals are integrated into an Integer Linear Programming formulation to assign per-expert bit-widths under a given budget. Extensive experiments show that MODE is particularly well-suited for MoE-MLLMs, limiting average performance loss to within 2.9% at W3A16, with larger gains at the extreme 2-bit setting.

### [216] [Noise-Driven Escape from Metastable Phases explains Grokking in Deep Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17120)
*Ibrahim Talha Ersoy,Karoline Wiesner*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了深度神经网络中，通过L2正则化强度的变化会导致一阶相变，每个相变标志着一个新可学习特征的出现。作者在线性DNN中证明，grokking（突然的延迟泛化）现象与一阶L2相变中的磁滞效应一致：模型被困在低精度的亚稳态中，只有SGD噪声驱动其跨越能垒才能逃逸，逃逸时间遵循阿伦尼乌斯标度。通过故意将模型困在亚稳态，作者在不同时间尺度上重现了类似grokking的延迟收敛。研究表明亚稳态的数量等于可学习特征的数量（即数据协方差奇异值的数量），并且这种机制可能也适用于一般的非线性DNN。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度神经网络尽管具有强大的泛化能力，但grokking现象（突然的延迟泛化）的起源尚不明确。作者希望揭示这一现象背后的物理机制，并理解L2正则化、一阶相变和磁滞效应在其中的作用。

Method: 作者在线性DNN框架下，通过分析L2正则化强度变化引起的一阶相变，引入磁滞效应来解释grokking。他们利用L2正则化故意将模型困在低精度亚稳态，观察SGD噪声如何驱动模型跨越能垒逃逸，并验证逃逸时间遵循阿伦尼乌斯标度。此外，还通过稀疏子采样重现了经典的grokking曲线。

Result: 1) 线性DNN中grokking与一阶L2相变中的磁滞效应一致；2) 模型在亚稳态中的逃逸时间遵循阿伦尼乌斯标度；3) 通过故意困住模型，在两个数量级的时间尺度上重现了grokking式延迟收敛；4) 亚稳态数量等于可学习特征数量（数据协方差奇异值数量）；5) 提供了证据表明该机制也可能适用于非线性DNN。

Conclusion: grokking现象的本质是DNN在L2正则化相变中的磁滞效应，模型被困在亚稳态中需要噪声驱动才能逃逸到高精度解。这一发现不仅解释了延迟泛化的起源，还为设计更高效的训练策略提供了理论指导。

Abstract: Deep neural networks (DNNs) exhibit first order phase transitions under variations of the L2 regularization strength, with each transition marking the onset of a new learnable feature. Below a critical regularization strength, all features are in principle learnable, but coexisting metastable states, separated by energy barriers, can trap the network and impede convergence. A strength of DNNs is their ability to generalize. But many open questions remain, among them the origin of so called grokking: the abrupt, delayed onset of generalization after prolonged apparent overfitting. We show for linear DNNs that grokking is consistent with hysteresis in first-order L2 phase transitions: using L2 regularization to engineer deliberate trapping, we demonstrate that a model in a low-accuracy metastable state escapes only when SGD noise drives it across an energy barrier, with escape times following Arrhenius scaling. We reproduce grokking-like delayed convergence across two orders of magnitude in escape time by deliberately trapping models in metastable phases. Using sparse sub-sampling we also reproduce the canonical grokking curve where test error eventually approaches the final training error. Our work suggests that the number of metastable states equals the number of learnable features -- one per singular value of the data covariance -- the potential for hysteresis grows naturally with task complexity. We provide evidence that the same mechanism likely operates in general nonlinear DNNs. Our results provide routes toward more efficient learning schemes.

</details>

The benchmark is reformulated as a graph in which nodes represent computational cells and edges encode transmissibility-based interactions enriched with geometric attributes. Directional transport arising from grid geometry, permeability contrasts, and geological heterogeneity is captured through an anisotropic message-passing mechanism, where interaction weights are computed via geometry-conditioned edge embeddings, biasing message aggregation toward physically relevant transport directions. Temporal evolution is modeled in latent space using an autoregressive residual formulation trained with multi-step supervision. The proposed model produces competitive forecasts of gas saturation and liquid-phase density, which are key indicators for CO$_2$ storage monitoring, with cumulative errors that remain moderate over extended forecasting horizons.

### [219] [Constrained Diffusion Models with Primal-Dual Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17192)
*Samar Hadou,Yigit Berkay Uslu,Alejandro Ribeiro*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出原始-对偶推理（PDI）方法，通过联合推断原始分布和对偶变量，在扩散模型中实现带有平均约束的熵正则化优化问题的约束采样。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有约束扩散采样方法通常先估计对偶乘子再冻结使用，无法动态适应采样过程中的约束变化。本文旨在解决这一局限，实现联合推断。

Method: PDI在逆向扩散每一步中：1) 使用当前对偶乘子对应的分数场去噪；2) 根据去噪样本的约束违背估计进行对偶上升更新乘子。训练单个对偶条件分数网络覆盖推理中遇到的所有吉布斯分布族。

Result: 理论上证明了推理轨迹中对偶变量的时间平均可收敛到对偶最优解的邻域，并通过调度依赖的稳定性因子界定了残差对偶失配对终端分布的影响。实验验证了在高斯混合、无线资源分配和投资组合管理任务上的有效性。

Conclusion: PDI通过动态联合推断的方式有效解决了带平均约束的扩散模型采样问题，兼具理论收敛保证和实际应用价值。

Abstract: This paper develops constrained diffusion models with primal-dual inference (PDI) to sample from optimal distributions of entropy-regularized optimization problems with \emph{average} constraints. We formalize constrained sampling in the Lagrangian dual domain, where the optimal distribution takes the form of a Gibbs distribution indexed by the optimal dual variable. Rather than estimating this dual multiplier before sampling and freezing it throughout generation, PDI jointly infers the optimal primal distribution and its parametrizing dual variable. Each reverse diffusion step denoises using the score field associated with the current multiplier and then updates the multiplier through dual ascent using the estimated constraint violation of the denoised samples. To enable this conditional score field, we train a single dual-conditioned score network over the family of Gibbs distributions induced by the dual variables encountered during inference. We prove that the time average of the dual variables generated along the inference trajectory converges to a neighborhood of the dual optimum and bound the effect of residual dual mismatch on the terminal distribution through schedule-dependent stability factors. We evaluate PDI on constrained sampling from a mixture of Gaussians, wireless resource allocation, and portfolio management.
